<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/w/index.php?title=lap-top&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="lap-top (page does not exist)">lap-top</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/lap#English" title="lap">lap</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">upper legs of a seated person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> +‎ <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/top#English" title="top">top</a></i>, modeled after <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/desktop#English" title="desktop">desktop</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈlæp.tɒp/</span></li>
<li><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r50165410">.mw-parser-output .k-player .k-attribution{visibility:hidden}</style><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: middle; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio (US)</td><td class="audiofile"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><span class="mw-tmh-player audio" style="width:175px;"><audio id="mwe_player_0_placeholder" preload="none" class="mw-file-element" width="175" style="width:175px;" data-durationhint="3" data-mwtitle="En-us-laptop.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" disabled="disabled" tabindex="-1"></audio><a class="mw-tmh-play" href="/wiki/File:En-us-laptop.ogg" title="Play media" role="button"><span class="mw-tmh-play-icon"></span></a><span class="mw-tmh-duration mw-tmh-label" aria-label="3 seconds">0:03</span></span></span></span></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:En-us-laptop.ogg" title="File:En-us-laptop.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈlæp.tɑp/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">laptop</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/laptops#English" title="laptops">laptops</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/laptop_computer" title="laptop computer">laptop computer</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2006</b>,  Corey Sandler,  <cite>Upgrading and Fixing Laptops For Dummies</cite>, page 8:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Over time, the difference in size between <b>laptops</b> and notebooks became a matter of no more than an inch or two in length and width, and a fraction of an inch in thickness.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> August 3,  “Revenge of the nerds”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Economist" class="extiw" title="w:The Economist">The Economist</a></cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.economist.com/news/finance-and-economics/21582512-explosion-start-ups-changing-finance-better-revenge-nerds">[1]</a></sup>, volume 408, number 8847:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Think of banking today and the image is of grey-suited men in towering skyscrapers. Its future, however, is being shaped in converted warehouses and funky offices in San Francisco, New York and London, where bright young things in jeans and T-shirts huddle around <b>laptops</b>, sipping lattes or munching on free food.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Dutch">Dutch</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Dutch">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">laptop</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_phonology" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch phonology">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Dutch_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Dutch pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈlɛp.tɔp/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgian_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Belgian Dutch">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Dutch_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Dutch pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈlɑp.tɔp/</span></li>
<li><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410"><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: middle; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio</td><td class="audiofile"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><span class="mw-tmh-player audio" style="width:175px;"><audio id="mwe_player_1_placeholder" preload="none" class="mw-file-element" width="175" style="width:175px;" data-durationhint="2" data-mwtitle="Nl-laptop.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" disabled="disabled" tabindex="-1"></audio><a class="mw-tmh-play" href="/wiki/File:Nl-laptop.ogg" title="Play media" role="button"><span class="mw-tmh-play-icon"></span></a><span class="mw-tmh-duration mw-tmh-label" aria-label="2 seconds">0:02</span></span></span></span></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:Nl-laptop.ogg" title="File:Nl-laptop.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li>
<li>Hyphenation: <span class="Latn" lang="nl">lap‧top</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl">laptop</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/laptops#Dutch" title="laptops">laptops</a></b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#diminutive" title="Appendix:Glossary">diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/laptopje#Dutch" title="laptopje">laptopje</a></b>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">laptop</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><span class="Latn" lang="en">computer with a clamshell design, portable and foldable</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Hungarian">Hungarian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Hungarian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">laptop</a></i>. It may also be considered as a <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#phono-semantic_matching" title="Appendix:Glossary">phono-semantic matching</a> of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">laptop</a></i>, its first element reinterpreted as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hungarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hungarian language">Hungarian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hu"><a href="/wiki/lap#Hungarian" title="lap">lap</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sheet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> due to its being slim.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_3">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Hungarian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Hungarian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">[ˈlɛptop]</span></li>
<li>Hyphenation: <span class="Latn" lang="hu">lap‧top</span></li>
<li>Rhymes: <a href="/wiki/Rhymes:Hungarian/op" title="Rhymes:Hungarian/op"><span class="IPA">-op</span></a></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Indonesian">Indonesian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Indonesian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">laptop</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_4">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indonesian_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Indonesian phonology">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">[ˈlaptɔp]</span></li>
<li>Hyphenation: <span class="Latn" lang="id">lap‧top</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="id">laptop</strong> (<i>first-person possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="id">laptop<a href="/wiki/-ku#Indonesian" title="-ku">ku</a></b>, <i>second-person possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="id">laptop<a href="/wiki/-mu#Indonesian" title="-mu">mu</a></b>, <i>third-person possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="id">laptop<a href="/wiki/-nya#Indonesian" title="-nya">nya</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">laptop</a></span>, <a href="/wiki/laptop_computer" title="laptop computer">laptop computer</a>: a portable computer that is small enough and light enough to be used on one's lap, but large enough to have an integrated keyboard.</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nb">laptop</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>definite singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/laptopen#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="laptopen">laptopen</a></b>, <i>indefinite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/laptoper#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="laptoper">laptoper</a></b>, <i>definite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/laptopene#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="laptopene">laptopene</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">laptop</a></span>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>2011</b>, <i>Madrugada</i> by Jan Mehlum, EbnPublish <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/8292526501" title="Special:BookSources/8292526501">→ISBN</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.co.uk/books?id=13V0DQAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PT245&amp;lpg=PT245&amp;dq=%22laptoper%22&amp;source=bl&amp;ots=BxeRLkg6hi&amp;sig=52CtpZUjC0NOcgNZLcuB-b0dcXA&amp;hl=no&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=2ahUKEwiqsanokeDdAhVLOMAKHe_HD3Q4RhDoATAFegQIBBAB#v=onepage&amp;q=%22laptoper%22&amp;f=false">[2]</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nb">Forretningsfolk, barnefamilier, unge kvinner med moderne klær, avanserte mobiltelefoner og <b>laptoper</b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Business people, families with children, young women with modern clothes, advanced mobile phones and <b>laptops</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_6">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=laptop&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="pt">laptop</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-pt p-form-of" lang="pt"><a href="/wiki/laptops#Portuguese" title="laptops">laptops</a></b>)
</p>
